Duarte le maloko a Mokgatlho wa Basadi wa ANC ba saenile phetišine go fetola Tselana ya William Nicole e e maphatha mane , Bokone ya Johannesburg , gonna ya Winnie Madikizela Mandela .
Ba kokoanetse kwa tselana kgolo ya William Nicol le N1 mo Pitori , kwa ba kopang tshegetso ya gore leina lefetolwe .
Khomoreiti Jessie Duarte , o eteletse pele letsholo la baagi mo Gauteng go tshegetsa phetolo ya leina la Tselana ya William Nicole go nna Winnie Madikizela Mandela le go thankgolola phetišine mo inthaneteng go fetola leina .
DA e tlhankgolotse phetišene mo inthaneteng go ganetsana le kakanyo ya go fetolwa ga leina , ka gore e tlile go nna kgato e e tlhokang madi a mantsi re le mo leroborobong la khorona .
Fa a bua le matshwithitshwithi go se gale , Duarte o rile : DA e iponetse mesaeno e le dikete di le nne kgatlhanong le didikadike tsa batho , a re bone b aba tlaa itlhaolang mo go ba bangwe botoka .
Batho ba Aforikaborwa ba tlile go fetola tsela e go nna Winnie Madikizela Mandela .
ANCWL e lopa tshegetso ya go fetola tsela ya William Nicol .
Ba kokoanetse kwa tselana kgolo ya William Nicol le N1 'mo Pitori , kwa ba kopang tshegetso ya gore leina lefetolwe .
Duarte o ne a neela morafe wa batho puo e se kgale , Duarte o rile : Batho ba le bantsi ba ba nnang mo ba tshela sentle , ga go na sepe se se fetogileng mo go bona .
Mme re tlile go fetola tsela e , re e bitsa , Winnie Madikizela Mandela .
Re tshwanetse go itebaganya le ntlha ya gore re netefatse fa ikonomi ya rona e laolwa ke Bantsho ba Maaforikaborwa .
Ga go a tshwanela gore le jaana ikonomi e santse e le mo diatleng tse di sele , ga tlhalosa Duarte .
Modulasetulo wa Lekoko la Bosetšhaba la ANC kwa Ekurhuleni Mzwandile Masina o tsentse boikuelo go Komiti Khuduthamaga ya Bosetšhaba go akanye sešwa ka ga tshwetso ya go sekegwa ga maloko .
Mokwaledi - Kakaretso wa ANC Ace Magashule o lebanwe ke ditatofatso tsa bosenyi , boferefere le go tlhatswa madi a seng mo molaong a golaganngwang le konteraka ya didikadike tsa dimilone tsa diranta go tlosa dithulelo tsa asebesetose mo matlong fa e ne e le Tonakgolo ya Foreisetata .
Magashule ke mongwe wa baetapele ba ANC ba ba neetsweng go fitlha kgwedi e ya fifing gore e be ba sekegwa go fitlha dikgetse tsa bona di konoseditswe .
Mo puong ya gagwe le babegadikgang tebang le matogwana a Makgotlha a ANC kwa Alberton ka Sontaga , Masina o rile Magashiule o tshwanetse go newa tšhono ya go tlhagisa letlhakore la gagwe .
Khomoreiti Ace ga a ise a bonwe molato .
Ke dumela gore o tshwanetse go newa tšhono ya go reetswa le gore go reetswe ka ga kgetse ya gagwe . Ga ke dumele gore re tshwanetse go rosa baeteledipele tiro mo Zoom .
Baetapele ba tshwanetse go nna fa fatshe , le go utlwana ka gonne ditlamorago tsa Nasrec di ka se ikgatolosiwe , a rialo Masina .
Re sa ntse re le foo , ANC kwa Ekurhuleni ba re ba tshosiwa ke gore molawana wa go sekegwa ga maloko o tlile go tlisa mathata mo mokgatlhong .
Go na gape le matshwenyego a gore tshwetso e e tlile go tlisa mathata mo tlhophong ya mokhanselara mo dikopanong tsa lekala .
Sedika sa Mmasepala wa Fezile Dabi wa ree tlile go thapola ANC fa Magashule a ka sekegwa .
Makala a a mo kgaolong a tsere kgato go ya pele ka go latofatsa Komiti Khuduthamaga ya Bosetšhaba ( NEC ) ka go ke tsaya letlhakore tebang le go tsenngwa tirisong ga tshwetso ya go sekegwa ga maloko .
Mmitsalekgotlha wa Kgaolo Jabu Sigasa a re makalana a lopa ka tshoganyetso Khansele ya Kakaretso ya Bosetšhaba go akanya sentle ka ga bokamoso jwa ga Magashule .
Mogokaganyimogolo wa kgaolo ya Fezile Dabi wa Lekoko la Bosetšhaba ( ANC ) Fezile Dabi kwa Foreisetata , Morulaganyi wa Kgaolo mo Foreisetata , Reagan Booysen , a re ba etetse makalana otlhe a ANC mo porofenseng go netefatsa fa Mokwaledi - Kakaretso wa lekoko Ace Magashule , a bona tshegetso ya maemo a a kwa godimo e Booysens a kayang fa e mo
tshwanela .
Kgaolo e , ya re e tlile go kgoreletsa Komiti Khuduthamaga ya Bosetšhaba ( NEC ) go emisa tshwetso ya go sekegwa .
Se se tla jaaka letsatsi la masomeamararo la paka e Magashule a e beetsweng gore a emele fa thoko ka ponyo ya leitlho .
Magashule o lebanwe ke ditatofatso tsa bosenyi gareng ga tse dingwe .
Booysens mo puong ya gagwe le ba bobegakgang kwa Parys , o rile : Re tlile go kgoreletsa tshwetso e ya [ go sekegiwa ] , re emetse letlha la bofelo re be re kgoreletsa tshwetso eo .
Modulasetulo le Tonakgolo ya maloba ya Lekoko la Bosetšhaba ( ANC ) , Supra Mahumapelo , a re ANC e gataka molaotheo .
Mahumaphelo a re ditshwetso dingwe tsa lekoko ga di inyalane le molao .
Puo ya gagwe le makala a ANC kwa Delareyville , Mahumapelo o tsentse boikuelo go ba Komiti Khuduthamaga ya Bosetšhaba ( NEC ) ya lekoko le le go tseleganya .
Go sekegiwa ga Mahumapelo go ne go kaiwa e le tharabololo , e e layang baetapele ba ANC b aba latofatswang ka bosenyi kgotsa bogodu jo bo tseneletseng go emela kwa thoko .
Dikarolo tse dingwe tsa ditharabololo ga di inyalane le molao e bile re tshwanetse go itshela moriti o o tsididi .
Go ya ka pono ya me jaaka SOR Mahumapelo go tswa wotong 6 , 7 , 12 , ka re karolo nngwe ya tshwetso eo ga e inyalane le molao e tshwanetse go emisiwa go fitlhela re ya kwa khonferenseng ya bosetšhaba e e latelang , o bua jalo .
Mahumapelo a re ba dirile kopo ya go sekegwa go beelwa kwa thoko .
Mahumapelo o tlatsa ka gore kemiso ya tshwetso ya go sekegiwa ga maloko e tlile go tlisa kamano e e siameng magareng ga maloko a ANC .
Fa o emisa dikarolo tsa ditshwetso tse di sa inya ; laneng le molao , ANC e boela ke dilo tse pedi : 1 ) ke go inyalana le tshwetso ya yona , ka fa go le lengwe , ke go inyalana le Molao wa Rephaboliki .
Se o tshwanetseng go se dira ke gore batho ba ba latofadiwang , ba ba tshwerweng , boeteledipele bo tshwanetse go tla le go tlhaloganya tsamaiso ya sepolotiki
Mahumapelo o sekegilwe nakwana mo ANC beke e e fetileng go ngangisana Komiti ya nakwana ya Porofense mo Bokonebophirima , yo a laetseng Meiyara wa Selegae wa JB Marks go rola tiro ka ntlha ya ditatofatso tsa bosenyi .
Theeletso ya gagwe ya dikgato - kgalemo e le ka Mosupologo le Labobedi .
Mahumapelo o loma tsebe makalana ka ga go sekegwa ga maloko a le mmalwa a a itsegeng a ANC .
Go ya ka sepolotiki le molao legae la Mokwaledi - kakaretso wa Lekoko la Bosetšhaba ( ANC ) Ace Magashule Fezile Dabi la re ba tlile go kgoreletsa Komiti Khuduthamaga ya Bosetšhaba ( NEC ) fa Magashule a ka sekegiwa .
Magashule ke mongwe wa baetapele ba ANC ba ba neetsweng go fitlha kgwedi e ya fifing gore e be ba sekegwa go fitlha dikgetse tsa bona di konoseditswe
Setlhopha sa tiro sa kgaolo sa re se etetse makalana a bakgaratlhi ba sepolotiki mo ANC le bokamoso jwa ga Magashule .
Bontsi jwa makala ba re ANC e tshwanetse go kgoreletswa to sireletsa Magashule gore a se ke a sekegwa ka ntlha ya fa a lebanwe ke ditatofatso tsa tsietso , bosenyi , le go tlhatswa madi a a seng mo molaong .
Makala a ANC a neetse ba RTT taelo , boeteledipele bo tshwanetse go netefatsa gore taelo e e ntseng jalo e tsenngwa tirisong
Re letetse fela letlha la bofelo mme re tlile go kgoreletsa tshwetso eo ka gonne re itse ditshwetso tse re di tsereng kwa Nasrec le makalana a bua ka kiletso e ka ntlha ya ditshwetso tse ba di tsereng , ga bua jalo Motlatsa Morulaganyi wa kgaolo , Reagan Booysens .
Makala a kwa Fezile Dabi a tsere kgato go ya pele ka go latofatsa Komiti Khuduthamaga ya Bosetšhaba tebang le go tsaya letlhakore ka ga tshwetso ya go sekegwa ga maloko .
Mogokaganyimogolo wa kgaolo Jabu Sigaga a re makalana a batla ka tshoganyetso gore Khansele ya Kakaretso ya Bosetšhaba go go akanya sentle bokamoso jwa ga Magashule .
Re tsenya boikuelo jwa tshoganyetso go NGC go nna fa fatshe kwa go tlaa kopanang makala a mangwe tebang le tshwetso e ya go sekegwa ga maloko .
Kgaolo ya Fezile Dabi e letleletse tshwetso ya Modulasetulo wa Porofense Sam Mashinini go dira boikuelo kgatlhanong le katlholo ya kgotlatshekelo go fedisa Komiti Khuduthamaga ya porofense .
Modulasetulo wa maloba wa ANC le Bokonebophirima Tonakgolo Supra Mahumapelo . O gorogile kwa Holong ya Toropo ya Delareyville fa a rulagantseng go loma makala ka ga gosekegiwa ga gagwe le maloko a mangwe a ANC ke Komiti ya nakwana ya Porofence .
O tshwaragane le Mokwaledi wa Lekgotla la Basadi la ANC , Bitsa Lenkopane , yo gape a lebanweng ke kgalemo .
Botokololo jwa ga Mahumapelo mo ANC bo emisitswe go sa le gale mo bekeng morago ga go bolelela Tona ya Mmasepala wa JB Marks , Kgotso Khumalo , gore a seke a sekegiwa ka ntlha ya tsietso le bonweenwee jo a latofadiwang ka bona .
Balatedi ba ga Mahumapelo ba gana nang ya banyana ka ga go sekegiwa ga gagwe .
Mahumapelo ke tokololo ya Palamente e nil eke mongwe wa ba le batlhanomo Bokonebophirima ba maloko a ANC , go akaretsa Tonakgolo Job Mokgoro , ba ba lebanweng ke ditatofatso tsa bosenyi mo porofenseng .
Mokgoro , le fa go ntse jalo , o kaile fa a sa tle go nna karolo ya kopano ya gompieno .
Botokololo jwa ANC jwa ga Tonakgolo bo emisitswe morago ga go sa lateleng taelo ya ANC la nako ya ditlhopho tsa modulasetilo yo mo ntšhwa wa ditulo tsa peomolaong mo porofenseng .
Puso ya KwaZulu - Natal ya re e tlhotlheletsa letsholo la moento wa COVID - 19 e bile seo se mo tseleng ya go fitlhelela maitlhomo a lona , go entilwe badiri ba lefapha la pholo ba feta 50 000 ba maokela a sephira le ba semmuso .
Tonakgolo Sihle Zikalala o dirile kitsiso kwa Durban ka Sontaga .
Zikalala o solofela gore mo legatong la bobedi la lenaneo la go entiwa fa kgwedi ya Lwetse e ya fifing , porofense e tshwanetse ya bo e entile batho ba lekana le didikadike / dimilone di le tharo .
KwaZulu - Natal go na le mafelo a le masomearobongwe le batho ba feta dikete di le supa ba katiseditsweng go enta .
Porofense e supile mafelo a a magolo a moento mo Pietermaritzburg le kwa Durban .
Maikaelelo bona ke go dira meento e le masomeamararo ka beke .
Setlhopha sa KwaZulu - Natal se file PSL go fitlha ka 10am go araba kgotsa go lebagana le dikgato tsa semolao mme ka mokgwa o dilo di emeng ka ona , liki jaanong e ineetse ka mo tlase ga kgatelelo .
Liki e nnile bonako go tlhagisa gore go busediwa morago e ne e se kamogelo ya gore Royal AM e ne e nepagetseng mo tlhalosong ya bona ya katlholo ya ga Nyathi .
Baemedi ba semolao ba liki ga jaana ba arabile Royal AM mme ba tlhalosa gore go bonala go na le kganetsano e e mabapi le taelo ya ga Moatlhodi Nyathi ka Mosupologo .
Modirelwa wa rona o amogela tlhaloso e e fetileng , fa modirelwa wa lona ena a amogela tlhaloso e e tlileng kwa morago .
Liki e tlhalositse gore e ikaelela go dira kopo kwa kgotlatshekelong e e potlakileng gore go ntshiwe taelo ya motheo ya ga Moatlhodi Nyathi le kgapelothoko ya yona .
Gore go kgone go rarabololwa kgotlhang e e mabapi le tlhaloso e e lolameng ya ga Nyathi J , modirelwa wa rona o ikaeletse go dira kopo go kgotlatshekelo e e kwa godimo e e potlakileng ka ntlha ya taelo ya go bolela gore section 18 ( 1 ) e tswenngwe tirisong gore tiro le tiriso ya taelo ya ga Nyathi AJ e emisitswe ka kopo ya khunologo ya go ikuela .
Ka fa letlhakoreng le lengwe , modirelwa wa rona o tla kopa gore tiro le tiriso ya taelo ya ga Nyathi J e sekegiwe go ya ka section 18 ( 2 ) .
Dipampiri di tlaa romelwa go modirelwa wa lona ka imeile kwa dikantorong tsa lona jaaka babueledi mo ntlheng e , ka bonako jo bo kgonegang , mo tsamaong ya letsatsi .
Ka Lamatlhatso , katlholo e ne ya neelwa mo kgaisanong ya Glad Africa e e akaretsang Sekhukhune United , Polokwane City le Royal AM , kwa kgotlatshekelo e e kwa godimo kwa Johannesburg .
Topotuelo ya go sekaseka tsereganyo e e neetsweng ke Epstein SC ka di 19 Motsheganong 2021 ga e a amogelwa , buisa go ya ka karolo ya taelo ya kgotlatshekelo e e kwa godimo .
Ga latela motshameko o mo go ona ba tlhotsweng 1 - 0 , Ba Bina Noko , jaaka Sekhukhune United e itsege , ba tsentse ngongorego mo PSL DC , ba ngongoregela gore City e paletswe ke go akaretsa batshameki ba dingwaga tse di kwa tlase ga 23 ba le tlhano mo setlhopheng sa bona go ya ka melawana ya PSL .
Fa PSL DC e sena go bona Polokwane City molato le go gogela morago dintlha di le tharo tse ba neng ba di fitlhetse kgatlhanong le Sekhukhune , ba tsere tshwetso ya go se abele setlhopha se se ganetsang dintlha tseo , jaaka ba ne ba dirile mo mabakeng a a tshwanang a mo nakong e e fetileng .
Se se dirile gore Ba Bina Noko ba tlhatlhele kgetse kgatlhanong le tshwetso ya PSL DC . Dipholo tse e neng e le tshwetso e e dirilweng ke botsereganyi kgatlhanong le dintlha di le tharo le dino di le tharo go United malatsi a le mmalwa pele ga karolo ya bofelo ya metshameko e e tla swetsang gore ke setlhopha sefe magareng ga Royal AM le United se
se tla amogelang tlhatloso go ya kwa metshamekong ya DSTV .
Le fa go ntse jalo , Komiti khuduthamaga ya PSL , morago ga moo , e ne ya botsolotsa tshwetso ya katlholo , ya go gana go abela Sekhukhune United dintlha le dino .
Tshwetso e , e ne e tshwanetse go tswela Royal AM , e e tseneng mo motshamekong wa makgaola kgang kgatlhanong le Cape Town All - Stars mosola kwa godimo ga kgaolo ya ntlha .
Ba ne ba tswelela go fenya motshameko wa bona wa bofelo morago ga go newa penalethi e e boleta mo kgatong ya bofelo ya motshameko wa bona le mororo PSL e sa ba neela sekgele le mmentlele mme ba kaya fa se e le ka ntlha ya fa ba ne ba neetswe dipampiri tse di tswang kwa kgotlatshekelo .
Basimolodi ba bagolo ba thonamente , North Macedonia ga ba ka fa tlase ga kgatelelo epe ya go fitlhelela Euro 2020 , ya ba le 16 ba bofelo pele ga thulano ya bona e e botlhokwa ya setlhopha sa C le Ukraine ka Labone , mokatisi Igor Angelovski o buile jalo .
Ditlhopha ka bobedi di lebeletse phenyo ya tsona ya ntlha morago ga fa setlhopha sa kwa Ukrain se sena go nosa nno mo motshamekong o mo go on ba fentsweng 3 - 2 ke Netherlands , fa North Macedonia e latlhegetswe 3 - 1 kgatlhanong le Austria .
Okare ke motshameko wa bofelo mo matlhakoreng a mabedi
Le rona re ne re na le tsholofelo ya natlafatsa letlhakore la rona la kgwebo mme tshwanetse go nna re tlhomile mogopolo mo go seo .
Re e kopakopanya le ditlhopha tse di gaisang tsa kwa Europe .
Angelovski ga a a bua sepe ka ga diphetogo tse di ka diragalang kwa tshimolong le mo popegong ya setlhopha .
Banka e e tshesane ga e mo fe ditshono di le dintsi thata , le mororo Ivan Trickovski e le ena a batliwang go gaisa Aleksandar Trajkovski kwa pele .
Mosireletsi Stefan Ristovski o rile mowa wa setlhopha o ne o santse o le kwa godimo .
Re ka se letle go fenngwa gangwe fela go senye maikutlo a rona le go nna mo Euros lwa ntlha .
Ga go na nako e ntsi ya kutlobotlhoko kgotsa ya keteko , le fa go ka diragala eng . a rialo .
Re lebagane le motshameko o o thata mme re tshwanetse go tlhagisa tiro e e kwa godimo gore re kgone go bona tšhono ya go fenya .
Fa go tliwa mo tshireletsong , go tlaa tlhokega basireletsi ba le babedi go sireletsa kgatlhanong le setlhopha sa kwa Ukraines .
North Macedonia e tlaa tshameka kgatlhanong le Netherlands mo setlhopheng sa bofelo kwa Amsterdam ka Mosupologo , fa Ukraine yona e tlaa tshameka kgatlhanong le Austria kwa Bucharest .
Ukraine ga e kitla e tlhoka tlhotlheletso e e kwa godimo fa ba tsena mo motshamekong wa Euro 2020 , setlhopha C le North Macedonia ka Labone , mme ba ikutlwa ba na le maikutlo a a siameng le fa ba ne ba latlhegetswe mo motshakong wa bona wa pulo kgatlhanong le go Netherlands , tlhogo ya bakatisi Andriy Shevchenko o buile jalo ka Laboraro .
Ukraine e ikarabetse ka 2 - 0 go Dutch ka Sontaga mme ba ne ba lebega ba le malala a laotswe go iponela maleka , fela nno ya ga Denzel Dumfries e ba siile ba iphotlhere .
Re tlhaloganya setlhopha ka botlala .
Re a itse gore ke ditiro dife tse di re emetseng mme ga go botlhokwa gore re bue go feta foo .
Batshameki ba setlhopha ba baakanya ditlhaloganyo tsa bona , Shevchenko o boleletse babegakgang .
Se ke thonamente e e botlhokwa thata .
Ga e se ngwaga le ngwaga mo re fitlhang kwa maemong a setlhopha mo metshamekong ya makgaolakgang ya kwa Europe , ka jalo motshameki mongwe le mongwe o tlhaloganya botlhokwa jwa motshameko mongwe le mongwe mme o na le maikarabelo a motshameko wa gagwe le motshameko wa setlhopha ka kakaretso .
Ka jalo ga re tlhoke mafoko go tlaleletsa .
North Macedonia e fentswe 3 - 1 ke Austria mo motshamekong wa bona wa ntlha mme ba dutse mo maemong a a kwa tlase ga Ukraine .
Shevchenko o rile maikutlo mo setlhopheng sa gagwe a ne a le mantle mme ga ba kitla ba nyatsa ditlhopha tse di tlaa tshamekang kgatlhanong le ba bona , tse di tshamekang thonamente ya tsona ya ntlha jaaka naga e e ikemetseng .
Re itse gore re tlhaetse go le gonnye fela gore re kgone fitlhelela dipholo tse di itumedisang .
Tsibogo go tswa go setlhopha e ne e itumedisa .
Re nnile le nako e e itumedisang mme re na le tsholofelo mo motshamekong o o tlang , Shevchenko o buile jalo .
North Macedonia ke setlhopha se se tshwanelwang ke tlotlo .
Ba na le botho , mokgwa wa bona wa go tshameka mme ba tlhasela sentle .
Mo dingwageng di le dintsi tse di fetileng , ba nnile le metshameko e e siameng , e mo go yona ba fentseng ditlhopha tse di kwa godimo .
Ka jalo re tshwanetse go nna kelotlhoko thata ka tlhaselo ya bona .
Mokatisi wa Turkey Senol Gunes o supile batshameki ba ba rileng ka monwana ka ntlha ya diphoso tse ba di dirileng kwa tshimologong ya Euro 2020 , morago ga gore phenyo ya Wales ya 2 - 0 ka Laboraro e ba sie ba sena ntlha morago ga metshameko e mebedi .
Morago ga go latlhegelwa 3 - 0 go Italy mo motshamekong wa setlhopha sa A , Turkey e wetse tlase morago ga gore Aaron Ramsey le Connor Roberts ba nosetse Wales kwa lebaleng la metshameko la Bakus .
Ga ke akanye gore re amogetseng letshogo le re nnileng le lona ka motshameko wa ntlha ( kgatlhanong le Italy ) , Gunes a rialo .
Segolo bogolo ka halofo ya ura ya ntlha , ke akanya gore re ne re santse re akantse motshameko o fetileng .
Le fa go le jalo , re dirile tshimologo e e siameng mo halofong ya bobedi mme motshameko o ne wa laolwa ke rona nakwana , go fitlha re simolola go dira diphoso gape , mokatisi yo o nang le maitemogelo o buile jalo .
Turkey , e e tla lebaganang le Switzerland mo motshamekong wa bona wa bofelo wa setlhopha , ba lekile go nosa dino di le tlhano mo metshamekong ya bona e mebedi ya ntlha ya thonamente mme ba feleleditse ba sa nosa le fa e nngwe ya dino tseo .
Ga ke gakologelwe re dira diphoso tse dintsi jaana mo go fetiseng kgwele , le eseng .
Fa o latlhegelwa ke kgwele bonolo jalo , mme o na le bothata jwa go e busetsa gape kwa go wena , ga go gakgamatse gore o tlaa nna le bothata . Gunes a tlaleletsa .
Fa a bodiwa gore a maano a gagwe a nnile le seabe mo ditatlhegelong tse pedi tse , Gunes o rile : """" O ka tsenya go tlhoka maitemogelo mo kgannyeng e , tlhaelo ya maatla a mmele , le kitso ya go lwantsha batshameki ka bongwe ka bongwe . """"
Kwa bokhutlong jwa letsatsi , ke etse tlhoko morwalo o o relweng ke setlhopha mo magetleng a bona , mme re paletswe ke go tiisa nonofo ya bona ka boikanyego gore re kgone go ba rola morwalo o .
Ke tsaya maikarabelo ka botlalo .
Botlhe ke batshameki ba ba siameng , mme re ne re solofetse go le gontsi go tswa mo go bona .
Ga go siama gore re tshwaye batshemeki diphoso .
Italy e eteletse pele Setlhopha sa A ka dintlha di le thataro morago ga metshameko e mebedi mme ba eteletse kwa pele Wales ( nne ) , Switzerland ( nngwe ) le Turkey ( lefela ) .
Ba ka iponela maemo a a kwa godimo go feta ka go tshameka maleka mo motshamekong wa bona wa bofelo kgatlhanong le Wales ka Sontaga .
Italy ke yona setlhopha sa ntlha go fitlhelela kwa karolong ya 16 .

Mokatisi wa Switzerland Vladimir Petkovic o boleletse batshameki ba gagwe gore ba se ka ba bontsha Italy tlotla e e feteletseng mme ba nne le tumelo ya gore ba ka kgona go fenya fa ditlhopha tse di kopana mo thulanong ya dikgaisano tsa makgaolakgang tsa kwa Europe kwa Rome ka Laboraro .
Italy e kgapetse kwa thoko Turkey 3 - 0 mo kgaisanong ya ga go bula mo metshamekong ya bona ya bofelo e le 28 go tloga ka Lwetse 2018 .
Re tla dira se re tlwaetseng go se dira , e leng go tshameka motshameko wa rona , Petkovic o boleletse babegadikgang ka Labobedi .
Re tla tlotla Italy , fela e seng go feta selekanyo .
Ke bommamoratwa ba bagolo , e seng fela mo setlhopheng sa rona , mme mo kgaisanong eno ka kakaretso .
Rotlhe re bone boleng jo ba bo bontshitse kgatlhanong le Turkey .
Mme le rona le na le boleng e bile re ka ba gakgamatsa .
Re tla leka go fetola motshameko gore o direle rona mme re nne bonako go tlhasela le go tlhama tšhono .
Switzerland e tshamekile kgatlhanong le Belgium , Brazil , England le Spain mo dingwageng tse di fetileng , se Petkovic a reng se tshwanetse go ba naya lebaka le le isegang .
Ke solofela gore re tla bontsha 120 % , fela jaaka re dirile kgatlhanong le ditlhopha tse dingwe tse dikgolo .
Re tla tlhoka go nna botoka go feta ka mokgwa o re leng ka teng .
Re tla tshwanelwa ke go nna le maikaelelo a magolo , re taboge thata mme re nne batshameki ba ba siameng .
Ka jalo re ka fenya , o ne a bolela jalo .
Re tlhoka go tshameka motshameko wa rona le go nna kotsi mo karolong ya bofelo ya boraro .
Re tshwanetse go ela tlhoko maItaly a a rileng , mme gape re nne le nnete mo go rona .
Tla re tseye dilo ka bongwe ka bongwe ka nako , ga re kitla re iketelela kwa pele , a tlaleletsa .
Go botlhokwa thata go naya 120 % , ka tshimologo e e ntle ya XI e e leng teng .
Re solofela gore re tla tlhagisa tiragalo e kgolo le go fenya kgaisano e go netefatsa gore re ka kgona go ya kwa legatong le le latelang .
Mokatisi wa Italy Roberto Mancini a re setlhopha sa gagwe se tlaa tokafala fela pele ga motshameko wa kgaisano wa bobedi kgatlhanong le Switzerland , le fa ba dirile tshimologo e e batlileng e le botoka thata mo thulanong ya bona ya pulo le Turkey mo bekeng e e fetileng .
Motshameko wa Turkey o ne o le boima thata , Mancini o boleletse khonferense ya dikgang .
Mme e rile fa sena go nosa , ba lokologa .
Re tla tshwanelwa ke go fenya e e latelang mme fa go kgonega , re fenye e nngwe gape e e latelang .
Re tshwanetse go dira bojotlhe jwa rona .
Ke na le tsholofelo .
Se , ke setlhopha se se gaisang se se ka tokafalang . .
Fa batsayadibetšhe ba maasemane ba ka re ( Italy ke yona mmamoratwa ) , re a amogela ka gore ba dira sentle , mme fela mo kgaisano e sa ntse e le telele .
Re na le tiro e ntsi e re tshwanetseng go e dira .
Phenyo ya Switzerland e tlaa dira gore Italy e nne yona setlhopha sa ntlha go fitlhelela dikgato tsa peletsontle tsa EURO 2020 , ka motshameko o le mongwe wa setlhopha sa A o santse o tlile go tshameka .
Le fa go ntse jalo , Italy e fentse metshameko e mebedi ya pulo gabedi fela mo dikgaisanong tsa makgaolakgang tswa kwa Europe di le robonngwe tse di fetileng , ba dirile jalo ka 2000 le 2016 , mme Mancini ga a tseye Switzerland botlhofo .
Ba ka gale mo setlhopheng sa kgwele ya dinao ya maemo a a kwa godimo mo lefatsheng , ba na le batshameki ba ba nang le bokgoni , mme gape ba na le mokatisi yo o itseng Italy sentle ka ntlha ya fa a e katisitse mo nakong e e fetileng .
Go ka nna bokete , mme re tlaa tlhoka go nna mo maemong a a kwa godimo .

Mo Lekgotla la Boditšhabatšhaba la Kerikete ( ICC ) le itumelela gore WTC e tlisitse kgatlhego e ntsi mo go tsa kirikete .
Go ne go le mo pepeneneng gore kgatlhego mo motseletseleng o o rileng e ne e se mo ditlhopheng tse pedi tse di amegang fela , CEO ya ICC ya nama o sa tshwere Geoff Allardice o boleletse kwa khonferense ya dikgang ka Mosupologo .
E ne e tswa go lefatshe la kirikete lefatshe ka bophara .
Mme ke akanya gore go tlisa bokao jwa mofuta o mo kiriketeng ke kgato e e kwa pele .
Batlhankedi ba kwa Japan ba ba laolang melawana ya coronavirus , ba tla tshwara khonferense ya dikgang moragonyana ka Laboraro .
Japan e ikaelela go tswelela pele ka tshitshinyo e e tla letlang babogedi ba ba fitlhang go 10 . 000 ka palo kgotsa 50 % ya go tlala ga mafelo , nngwe le nngwe fela e e leng nnye , kwa meletlong ka nako ya metshameko , dikgang tsa Kyodo di buile jalo ka Labobedi thapama , di nopola metswedi e mengwe ya puso .
Babogedi ba kwa ntle ba setse ba ileditswe go ya kwa tshimologong ya diolimpiking ka di 23 tsa kgwedi ya Phukwi .
Barulaganyi le batlhankedi ba mmuso kwa Japane ba rile ba tla tswelela go lebelela melawana ya coronavirus go netefatsa metshameko e e babalesegileng le e e sireletsegileng , le gore tshwetso ya babogedi e tlaa dirwa mo kgweding eno .
Tona ya ikonomi kwa Japan Yasutoshi Nishimura le mogakolodi yo o kwa godimo wa puso Shigeru Omi ba tla tshwara khonferense ya dikgang e e kopanetsweng ka Laboraro , kantoro ya kabinete e buile jalo .
Nishimura le Omi ba tlaa bua ka ga dikarabo tsa puso mabapi le coronavirus ka kopano ya bona ka Laboraro , Ofisi ya kabinete e buile jalo , mme ga e a tlamela dintlha tse dingwe le nako ga e ise e bewe .
Tokyo , Osaka le ditoropo tse dingwe di le robedi di tlaa tswelela go nna ka fa tlase ga maemo a tshoganyetso a a tla khutlang ka Seetebosigo 20 .
E ne e le motshameko o o boima mme re iponetse dintlha di le tharo .
Go ne go le botlhokwa go fenya le go simolola kgaisano ka boikanyo mme jaanong re batla go tswelela ka go fenya , go bua Ronaldo .
Mokatisi wa Portugal Fernando Santos o a tlaleletsa : Fa re ne re nositse kwa tshimologong , go ne go tla nna bonolo mo go rona .
Re latlhegetswe ke ditšhono di le mmalwa mme ra nna le dinako tsa go tlhobaela , re kgonne go itsotsoropanya gape le go fetsa motshameko sentle .
Motshamekapele Adam Szalai o ne a tshosetsa Hungary , fa a ne a latlhela kgwele ka tlhogo mo diatleng tsa ga Rui Patricio nakonyana pele ga nako ya go ikhutsa mme a leka motshwaradino gape mo halofong ya bobedi .
Mosireletsi wa kwa Portugal yo o nang le maitemogelo , Pepe o batlile go nosa kwa tshimologong ya karolo ya bobedi mme a kgorelediwa ke Gulacsi yo o dulang a le malala a laotswe , yo morago ga moo o neng a thibela tlhaselo e e tswang kwa go Fernandes .
Kemedi ya Hungary Szabolcs Schon o ne a tlisa matlhagatlhaga kwa lebaleng la metshameko mo motsotsong wa bo 80 fa thago ya gagwe e ne kgabola mo go Patricio mme rramela o ne a tsholetsa folaga ya gagwe ka bonako go emisa keteko .
Tiragalo e kgoba marapo ka metlha .
Re sireleditse sentle , setlhopha sotlhe se dirile sentle mme re ntshitse bojotlhe jwa rona , go buile mosireletsi wa kwa Hungary Attila Szalai .
Hungary e tla kopana le bommampodi ba lefatshe ba France mo nakong e e tlang kwa Puskas Arena , fa Portugal yona e tlaa lebagana le Germany kwa Munich .
Tonakgolo ya kwa Hungary e e ratang kgwele ya dinao Viktor Orban o ne a na le maikaelelo a go tlatsa lebala le le ntšhwa le le phatsimang , le le butsweng ka 2019 , jaaka a batla go itsege thata pele ga ditlhopho tse di tlang .
Orban , yo o neng a a le kwa motshamekong , o dirisitse dibilione tsa di euro tsa matlole a puso go tlhabolola didiriswa tsa kgwele ya dinao mme o ne a tshwaiwa diphoso ka go baya matlole a motshameko wa kgwele ya dinao kwa pele ga a tlhokomelo ya boitekanelo , segolobogolo jaaka leroborobo le tlhasetse .
Fa naga e sena go fenya lekhubu la bobedi la coronavirus , ka dikgetse tse dintšhwa tse di dutseng go 100 go ya go di le 200 mo bekeng e e fetileng ,
re leboga moento ka se , e kile ya bo e na le dipalopalo tse di kwa godimo tsa dintsho tsa COVID - 19 lefatshe ka bophara , tsa batho ba le 100 , 000 go ya ka tshedimosetso ya kwa Unibesithi ya John Hopkins
Go tswa ga Germany mo logatong lwa ntlha lwa Sejana sa Lefatshe sa 2018 go bakile tlhabololo ya setlhopha .
Mo kgaisanong ya gagwe ya bofelo pele a rola tiro morago ga dingwaga di le 15 , Loew o ne a gopola gore go lelekiwa ga bangwe ba batshameki morago ga tlhakatlhakano e e tlhodilweng ke leroborobo la COVID - go kaya gore setlhopha se reteletswe ke go bona dipholo tse di itumedisang .
Jaaka bommampodi ba lefatshe Thomas Mueller le Mats Hummels ba boetse mo setlhopheng morago ga dingwaga di le pedi , Germany e tla tsewa jaaka setlhopha se se nang le maitemogelo fa ba kopana baagisani ba bona ba ba nang le maatla .
Se Germany e tlaa tlhokang go se dira pele ke go tiisa tshireletso ya bona kgatlhanong le batshameki ba kwa pele kwa France , ba ba itsegeng e le bona ba ba itlhomileng kwa pele mo lefatsheng mo nakong eno .
France e ka bo e se bommampodi ba lefatshe ba fa ba ne ba se na basireletsi ba maemo a a kwa godimo , Go buwa Timo Werner wa kwa Germany .
Batshameki ba ba lebaganang le ba bangwe ka bongwe ka bongwe jaaka NGolo Kante kgotsa Benjamin Pavard .
Go na le lebaka la gore goreng go na le bommamoratwa ba thonamente .
Mme mo go tlhaseleng boraro jo ( Kylian ) Mbappe , ( Antoine ) Griezmann le ( Karim ) Benzema ba kwa maemong a a kwa godimo .
Fa o na le batshameki ba ba tshwanang le bao mo setlhopheng , go a itumedisa .
Benzema o fetsa go nna botoka morago ga kgobalo e nnye e a e boneng kwa motshamekong wa botsalano o mo go ona ba fentseng Bulgaria ka Labobedi mme o itekanetse gore a ka tshameka motshameko wa pulo .
Re tshwanetse go bona gore ke eng se se botlhokwa mo go rona , se re se tlhokang le gore maatla a rona a fa kae , go bua mothusa mokatisi kwa Jeremane , Marcus Sorg .
Sa bobedi , re tshwanetse go bona gore re ka tlosa jang setlhopha sa France mo motshamekong .
Re tshwanetse go leka , le kgatlhanong le France go tsenya maatla a rona mo lebaleng la motshameko .
Kwa bokhutlong jwa letsatsi , e ka nna seemo se le sengwe se se ka sireletsang katlego ya setlhopha , Sorg o buile jalo .
Ke ka moo go leng botlhokwa gore re dire tiro ya rona , mme batshameki ba rona ba tlhalogantse seo .
Christian Eriksen wa kwa Denmark a re o ikutlwa a siame mo tlase ga maemo a a leng mo go ona mme o bontshitse ditebogo ka melaetsa e a e amogetseng morago ga go itemogela bolwetse jwa pelo ka nako ya motshameko wa bona ya pulo ya Euro 2020 ka Lamatlhatso .
Re lebogela ditumediso le melaetsa ya lona e e monate go ralala lefatshe .
Go kaya go le gontsi mo go nna le ba lelapa la me , Eriksen o buile jalo mo posong e e kwadilweng mo porofaeleng ya setlhopha ya bosetšhaba ya Instagram e e tswileng ka Labobedi .
Ke siame ka fa tlase a maemo a .
Poso e , e ne e tsamaya le setshwantsho sa monna yo wa dingwaga di le 29 , a robetse mo bolaong kwa bookelong , a na le monyenyo mme a supa fa a siame .
Ke ikutlwa ke siame .
Jaanong , ke tla etleetsa basimane ba setlhopha sa Denmark mo metshamekong e e latelang . Tshamekelang Denmark yotlhe , a tlaleletsa .
Eriksen o ile a wa pelenyana ga nako ya go ikhutsa ka nako ya motshameko wa bona kgatlhanong le Finland mme o ne a isiwa bookelong morago ga go amogela CPR mo lebaleng .
Maabane , moemedi wa ga Christian Eriksen o rile motshameki yo o santse a tlhatlhobiwa mo go tseneletseng .
Rotlhe re batla go itse gore go diragetse eng ka ena , le ena fela jalo .
Dingaka di ntse di dira ditlhatlhobo tse di tseneletseng , go tla tsaya nako , kuranta ya kwa Italy , Gazzetta dello Sport ka Mosupologo e nopotse moemedi wa ga Eriksen , Martin Schoots jaaka a ne a bua .
Christian ga a itlhoboge .
Ene le ba lelapa la gagwe ba batla go romela ditebogo tsa bona go botlhe .
Motshameko wa setlhopha sa B o ne wa emisa mme wa tswelela gape morago ga ura le metsotso e le 45 . Finland e fentse ka 1 - 0 .
Tiragalo e tsosa dipotso ka ga tiro e ntsi e batshameki ba lebaneng le yona .
Eriksen o ne a tshameka motshameko wa gagwe wa bo 66 mo ngwageng fa e sale kgwele ya dinao e simolola morago ga go tswala ka ntlha ya leroborobo la coronavirus .
Melaetsa ya tshegetso e e lebisitsweng kwa go Eriksen a santse e thologela , go tswa mo motshamekong le go feta , sengwe se Schoots a rileng se thusitse go mo matlafatsa .
O ne a itumetse ka gonne o ne a tlhaloganya gore o dikaganyeditswe ke lorato lo lo kana kang , Schoots a tlaleletsa .
O amogetse melaetsa go tswa mo lefatsheng ka bophara .
O ne a gapilwe maikutlo thata ke melaetsa e e tswang kwa lefatsheng la Inter Milan ; E seng fela go tswa mo batshameki mmogo le ena ba a neng a bua le bona ka melaetsa , mme le balatedi .
Halofo ya lefatshe e ikgolagantse le rona , batho botlhe ba tshwenyegile .
Jaanong , o tshwanetse go ikhutsa .
Mosadi wa gagwe le batsadi ba gagwe ba na le ene .
Mme le fa go le jalo , o batla go tshegetsa tshameki mmogo le ena kgatlhanong le Belgium .
Hungary , e e tshamekang mo dikgaisanong tsa bona tsa bobedi tsa kwa Europe mo dingwageng di le 49 , ba tsewa jaaka batswantle , mo setlhopheng se se thata sa thonamente mme ba tlaa ba lebatsa se ka maina a bona a dinaledi le phisego e ba nang le yona .
Lefelo le le ntšhwa le le phatsimang la Puska ke lona fela lebala la metshameko le le kgonang go tsenya batho ba bantsi morago ga gore bothati jwa selegae bo dumele go ananya katogano ya batho ka melao e e gagametseng ya go tsena , e e tlhokang gore balatedi ba fane ka teko ya COVID - 19 e e se nang tshwaetsego .
Go raya gore Cristiano Ronaldo le Bruno Fernandes ba ka iphitlhela ba kgalwa ke matshwititshwiti a batho ba kwa Budapest mo motshamekong wa Labobedi , ba ba se kitlang ba kgotlelela diphoso dipe go tswa mo letlhakoreng la bona .
Ke ( Hungary ) setlhopha se se itekanetseng thata , se se kitlang se letla kgwele epe e tswa mo diatleng tsa bona e bile ba ka se ineele , go bua motshamekagare wa Portugal , Danilo .
Re itse mokgwa wa motshameko o re tshwanetseng re o lebelele go tswa mo go bona .
Re feditse setlha sotlhe re sa tshameke mo pele ga balatedi mme ga re sa tlhola re tlwaetse , fela go nna teng ga batho go tla dira gore motshameko o nne monate .
Hungary e tlabe e tletse matlhagatlhaga thata , mme ke nngwe ya mathata a re tlaa tshwanelang go samagana le i
Fa re beela kwa thoko ntwa ya batho , Portugal e tlile go lebagana le diteko tse di boima go tswa go Germany le France mme motshameko o ke tšhono e e molemo ya go iponela dintlha tse di tlaa ba thusang go tsena mo setlhopheng .
Portugal e itemogetse mathata kgatlhanong le Hungary kwa Euro 2016 , fa ba ne ba salela kwa morago makgetlho a le mararo pele ga ba boa ka maleka a 3 - 3 mme ba tsena mo dikgatong tsa peletsontle .
Letlhakore la ga Fernando Santos la Portugal ke lona le le tiileng mo selekanyong sa dingwaga di le tlhano , le humile ka batlhasedi ba ba tshwanang le Diogo Jota , Andre Silva , Joao Felix le Fernandes gammogo le Ronaldo yo o dulang a ikemiseditse .
Se ke setlhopha se se farologaneng , re na le batshameki ba ba botlana ba ba yang go tsenela thonamente ya bona ya ntlha ya boditšhabatšhaba , le fa e le gore phisego ya rona e santse e tlaa tshwana le ya kwa Euro 2016 , go tlaleletsa Danilo wa dingwaga di le 29 .
Setlhopha se se fetileng se ne se lomaganeng ka ba ne ba ntse ba tshameka mmogo mo nakong e telele . Le fa re le setlhopha se se potlana sa talente e e santseng e senoga , re setlhopha se se tshwaraganeng .
Rotlhe re akanya ka go tshwana mme go batla go fenya .
Re santse re le foo , Hungary , ga e bogale thata go tshwana le fa e ne e fitlhelela kwa kgatong ya bofelo ya peletsontle mo nakong e e fetileng , ba tshwere batho ba ba itsegeng thata jaaka Gabor Kiraly , Roland Juhasz le Zoltan Gera .
Gape ba latlhegetswe ke batshamekagare ba babedi ba bašwa , Dominik Szoboszlai le Zsolt Kalmar ka ntlha ya dikgobalo .
Fa a bodiwa gore ke motshameki ofe wa kwa Portugal o Hungary e tla be e tshwenyegile ka ena ka Labobedi , Rossi o ne a tshega .
Nka bala batshameki ba botlhe , o ne a bolelela babegakgape .
Fa ke ntsha leina le le lengwe fela ke tla be ke sa direle ba bangwe sentle .
Ba na le bokgoni jo bontsi mo dikarolong tsotlhe tsa lebala . .
Re tlhoka go thusana , re tshwanetse go netefatsa gore re mmogo , mme re tswale diphatlha fa gare ga mela .
Hungary e ikaegile thata mo tshireletsong e e popota le tlhaselo .
Maina a le mantsi a a sa tlwaelegang mo setlhopheng a kaya gore setlhopha se tla be se le matlhagatlhaga go feta se ba tshamekang kgatlhanong le sona , se se tshamekileng mo dithonamenteng tsa selegae le tsa boditšhabatšhaba .
Bagaka ba Bundesliga ba ba tshwanang le motshwaradino wa Leipzig e leng Peter Gulacsi ba tshamekela Hungary , ke batshameki ba ba popota le kwa ntle ga motshameki wa bona yo o tlhwatlhwa , Dominik Szoboszlai .
Re tshwanetse go diragatsa togamaano ya rona , bogolosegolo mo tshireletsong , ka gonne setlhopha se sa kwa Portugal se matlafetse le feta sa ngwaga wa 2016 , o buile jalo .
Hungary le Portugal di tshamekile mengwe ya metshameko ya setlhopha e e itumedisang thata kwa Euro 2016 , kwa Hungary e neng e itlhomile kwa pele makgetlo a le mararo mme Portugal e lekanya dino lekgetlho lengwe lengwe , go akaretsa le dino di le pedi tse di nositsweng ke Cristiano Ronaldo .
Hungary e ne e itlhomile kwa pele mo setlhopheng pele ga go latlhegelwa ka 4 - 0 kgatlhanong le Belgium mo karolong ya 16 fa Portugal yona e ikgapetse sekgele .
Ditlhopha di le robedi di tlaa tsenela dikgaisano tsa sekgele mo setlheng se se latelang .
